    SELECT r0."Id", r0."CategoryId", r0."ClauseIndex", r0."ClauseText", r0."Confidence", r0."CreatedAt", r0."IsActive", r0."Keywords", r0."Priority", r0."ReviewId", r0."Sentiment", r0."SentimentScore", r0."Suggestion", r0."Summary", r0."UpdatedAt", r2."Id" AS "Id0", r2."CreatedAt" AS "CreatedAt0", r2."DepartmentId", r2."IsActive" AS "IsActive0", r2."Key", r2."Keywords" AS "Keywords0", r2."Name", r2."UpdatedAt" AS "UpdatedAt0"
    FROM "ReviewAnalyses" AS r0
    LEFT JOIN (
        SELECT r1."Id", r1."CreatedAt", r1."DepartmentId", r1."IsActive", r1."Key", r1."Keywords", r1."Name", r1."UpdatedAt"
        FROM "ReviewCategories" AS r1
        WHERE r1."IsActive"
    ) AS r2 ON r0."CategoryId" = r2."Id"
    WHERE r0."IsActive"
) AS s ON r4."Id" = s."ReviewId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT r3."Id", r3."CreatedAt", r3."FileType", r3."FileUrl", r3."IsActive", r3."OcrText", r3."ReviewId", r3."UpdatedAt"
    FROM "ReviewAttachments" AS r3
    WHERE r3."IsActive"
) AS r5 ON r4."Id" = r5."ReviewId"
LEFT JOIN (
    SELECT a."Id", a."AssignedTo", a."CreatedAt", a."DepartmentId", a."DueDate", a."IsActive", a."ReviewId", a."Status", a."Title", a."UpdatedAt"
    FROM "ActionItems" AS a
    WHERE a."IsActive"
) AS a0 ON r4."Id" = a0."ReviewId"
ORDER BY r4."Id", s."Id", s."Id0", r5."Id"
